Hi everyone :)

Please feel free to forward this wherever you think it might be  
useful. This email sends it to grrltalk (since it's the busiest  
Linuxchix list), GNOME-Women and Ubuntu-Women. Thanks to Barry Warsaw  
of Mailman for the heads-up.

Go for the prize, chix! :D

If the lists strip the attachment, the info is at:
http://www.pizzigatiprize.org/

>

> see is more applications from women open source developers.  I hope  
> you don't mind me asking you to help spread the word to any open  
> source communities you might be involved with.
>

> great opportunity.
